Google <span class=\"match\">Chrome</span>   Sling TV is supported on the most recent ... recent version of Google <span class=\"match\">Chrome.</span> Normally, Google <span class=\"match\">Chrome</span> updates automatically. If ... browser to watch Sling TV, open Google <span class=\"match\">Chrome.</span> \u00a0  In the top-right corner, click on ... Settings icon.    Then click Update Google <span class=\"match\">Chrome.</span> If you do not see this option, this means","type":"ARTICLE","url":"/en/support/solutions/articles/33000218993-how-do-i-check-for-an-update-of-my-sling-tv-app-","source":{"article":{"art_type":null,"created_at":"2018-02-28T18:14:22-07:00","desc_un_html":"  Many of the devices and platforms that support Sling TV normally update apps automatically. If you still need to update, choose your device below for step-by-step instructions on how to do so:  \u00a0  If you don't see your device listed here, please refer to the manufacturer's instructions for how to update apps.     Amazon Fire Tablet   To find out if an update is available for Sling TV on your Amazon tablet, visit the App Store on your device. \u00a0Let's start by returning to your home screen.  \u00a0       \u00a0  Then tap\u00a0Apps.          Tap\u00a0Store, located on the top\u00a0right\u00a0corner of your screen, to open the App Store.       \u00a0     Once the App store has launched, look to the top\u00a0left\u00a0corner of your screen to locate the\u00a0menu\u00a0icon. \u00a0Click on the\u00a0menu\u00a0icon.  \u00a0          Scroll down within your menu until you land on\u00a0App Updates. Tap\u00a0App Updates. \u00a0All of your apps in need of an update will be available here.         If an update is available for Sling TV, tap the\u00a0Update\u00a0button located beside the Sling TV app details.        Tap Update\u00a0to being installing the update   Once the installation process is complete click\u00a0Open, located where\u00a0Update\u00a0was previously. \u00a0Your Sling TV App will launch. Return to your stream and enjoy! \u00a0        Apple TV  Your Apple TV is set to automatically update your applications. If you turned this function off, return to the App Store and select Sling TV. If an update is available, select Update.  Android Device   Typically, your Android device will launch a pop-up window notifying you of an available update. \u00a0If you click\u00a0OK,\u00a0you will automatically be redirected to the Google Play Store. If you do not click\u00a0OK, you can still access the update. To do so, open the\u00a0Google Play Store.             Locate your Sling TV App by using the search engine.  \u00a0          If an update is available, you will see an\u00a0UPDATE button, as opposed to open. Click\u00a0UPDATE to begin the installation process.             Before the installation begins you must accept the Terms and Conditions. \u00a0Click\u00a0ACCEPT to continue with your update.             Allow the download and installation process to run its course.                  Once the update is complete, simply click\u00a0OPEN\u00a0to return to your stream!        Android TV   Typically, your Sling TV app will automatically update on your Android TV. If an update does not automatically occur, follow the steps below to check for and install any available updates. \u00a0  Return to your Android TV home screen, scroll\u00a0down\u00a0to\u00a0Apps, then find and launch the\u00a0Google Play Store.       \u00a0  Scroll\u00a0down\u00a0to\u00a0My Apps.       \u00a0  The top bar within\u00a0My Apps will display any available updates by app. Click on the Sling TV App if it is available under updates.   Now click\u00a0UPDATE.   Your Android TV will launch an App Permissions form. Press\u00a0Accept\u00a0to start the installation process.   Allow the download and installation process to run its course.   Once the update is complete, click\u00a0OPEN to launch your newly updated Sling TV app!          Google Chrome   Sling TV is supported on the most recent version of Google Chrome. Normally, Google Chrome updates automatically. If you still need to update your browser to watch Sling TV, open Google Chrome. \u00a0  In the top-right corner, click on the Settings icon.    Then click Update Google Chrome. If you do not see this option, this means you are on the latest version.  Finally, click relaunch.  To learn how to see what version of Google Chrome you are using, click here.   iOS Device   To check for, or install, an update temporarily leave the Sling TV app, then open your\u00a0App Store.             Look to the bottom right corner of your App Store to locate the\u00a0Updates\u00a0folder.             If an update is available for Sling TV it will be listed here. Simply click the\u00a0UPDATE\u00a0button, then allow the installation to run its course.           Roku   Typically your Sling TV app will automatically update on your Roku device. \u00a0If an update does not automatically occur follow the \u00a0steps below to check for and install any available updates.     Start by returning to your Roku home screen.          \u00a0Select Settings.  \u00a0\u00a0       Then System.          \u00a0Next, select System Update.             Click Check Now. \u00a0             Your Roku device will scan for any available updates across all applications.             If an updates is available, your Roku device will automatically install the update. \u00a0Once the update is complete click OK. \u00a0          Use the Home button on your remote to return to your home screen. Then, launch your Sling TV app and begin streaming.           Windows 10   Your Windows 10 device can automatically update applications the moment they become available. To enable automatic update, please follow the steps below.     To start, open the Windows Store.             Press, or click, the user icon near the search bar on the top-right corner of the page.             Press, or click, Settings from the drop down menu.             Under App updates\u00a0is Update apps automatically,\u00a0switch the toggle to the On\u00a0position.  *This should be the default setting on your Windows 10 device.             If you would prefer to check manually for app updates follow the steps below. \u00a0Open the Windows Store and click on the user icon. Now, press, or click, Downloads and updates.         Press, or click, the blue Check for updates\u00a0box, under the search bar.  *You can also check for updates for specific apps by visiting their page in the Windows Store. If you still need to update your browser to watch Sling TV, open Google Chrome. \u00a0</p><p dir=\"ltr\">In the top-right corner, click on the Settings icon.</p><p dir=\"ltr\"><a href=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/4YvyHMA-n1mNsA0uo31mUA2YLIwS-ljUWhJ3dcgT6qaQ5JeE8o4DM3wGE5hJ1bY3s0DEHcge18eZ7-uQTFXeea13kxmtdi8Uv9Ex4eKsz13ZgfKzkk9EG-PtIxJL2vjw7Veh66m7\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><img src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/4YvyHMA-n1mNsA0uo31mUA2YLIwS-ljUWhJ3dcgT6qaQ5JeE8o4DM3wGE5hJ1bY3s0DEHcge18eZ7-uQTFXeea13kxmtdi8Uv9Ex4eKsz13ZgfKzkk9EG-PtIxJL2vjw7Veh66m7\" style=\"width: 624px; height: 341px;\" class=\"fr-dii\" alt=\"image of google home page on chrome browser with menu highlighted\"></a><br><br>Then click Update Google Chrome. If you do not see this option, this means you are on the latest version.</p><p dir=\"ltr\">Finally, click relaunch.</p><p dir=\"ltr\">To learn how to see what version of Google Chrome you are using, click <a href=\"/support/solutions/articles/33000219672-how-do-i-check-if-i-m-using-the-most-recent-version-of-google-chrome-\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>.</p></div><h4><strong>iOS Device</strong></h4><div><p>To check for, or install, an update temporarily leave the Sling TV app, then open your<span>\u00a0</span><em>App Store</em>.</p><p><br></p><p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-fil\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000548/original/ap_Wp2QhV-ZNNvF2bgOQtydy-DieWZHDTQ.png?1532024673\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000548/original/ap_Wp2QhV-ZNNvF2bgOQtydy-DieWZHDTQ.png?1532024673\" data-fileid=\"46000000548\" data-uniquekey=\"1532023399954\" style=\"width: 498px; height: 374.504px;\" alt=\"image of iOS home screen with app store highlighted\"></p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p>Look to the bottom right corner of your App Store to locate the<span>\u00a0</span><em>Updates</em><span>\u00a0</span>folder.</p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-fil\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000549/original/-_f4pbVetknajKk5ihxcmTlbZRE8U9sUcA.png?1532024754\" style=\"width: 496px; height: 372px;\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000549/original/-_f4pbVetknajKk5ihxcmTlbZRE8U9sUcA.png?1532024754\" data-fileid=\"46000000549\" data-uniquekey=\"1532023399954\" alt=\"image of app store with updates highlighted\"></p><p><br></p><p>If an update is available for Sling TV it will be listed here. Simply click the<span>\u00a0</span><em>UPDATE</em><span>\u00a0</span>button, then allow the installation to run its course.</p><p><br></p><p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-fil\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000550/original/LzIcCw6A6LEt6GRsjaNc5bWB7AYxFgL8CQ.png?1532024776\" data-filelink=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000550/original/LzIcCw6A6LEt6GRsjaNc5bWB7AYxFgL8CQ.png?1532024776\" data-fileid=\"46000000550\" data-uniquekey=\"1532023399954\" style=\"width: 496px; height: 371.743px;\" alt=\"image of sling app selected with available update\"></p><p><br></p></div><h4><strong>Roku</strong></h4><div><p>Typically your Sling TV app will automatically update on your Roku device. \u00a0If an update does not automatically occur follow the \u00a0steps below to check for and install any available updates.</p><p><br></p><p>Start by returning to your Roku home screen.</p><p><br></p><p><img class=\"fr-dib fr-fil\" src=\"https://s3.amazonaws.com/cdn.freshdesk.com/data/helpdesk/attachments/production/46000000551/original/Nwo_B4WyiCZWtKf2vkVSxvkfvIuyykIDQQ.png?1532024919\" style=\"width: 575px; App and Device Issues\u00a0  Click an issue below to see more     Account Access Error on Android Mobile      Issue Description   Workaround (if available)       Users wanting to manage their subscription from a mobile app (iOS, Android) may see a \u00a0continuous looping error when attempting to sign in to their accounts.    This issue should be resolved in app version 6.18.  If available, please update your app.  Additionally, please visit sling.com/account and sign in to make changes to your subscription.       Report This Issue      Browser Full Screen      Issue Description   Workaround (if available)       Users watching in full-screen mode on Safari or Chrome browsers may see the browser revert to an in-window view, showing player controls.\u00a0       This issue should be resolved in a coming release.  In the meantime, users can view Sling in their browser with player controls, or watch on a different device.     Report This Issue      Error 8-12\u00a0      Issue Description   Workaround (if available)       Users receive error code 8-12 on Amazon and Android TV devices, as well as Google Chrome browsers.       This issue should be resolved in a coming release. In the meantime, please try restarting the app.  If you're experiencing this error while viewing in a browser, please update your browser.  If you're experiencing this error on MacOS, ensure your device is updated to at least MacOS version 10.10.X, and that your Google Chrome Browser is at least version 69.  For Amazon Fire users experiencing this issue, please update your Sling app. If this does not resolve the issue, try signing out of - and back in to - the Sling app. If you're still receiving the error, please restart your device.       Report This Issue      Shows being cut off         Issue Description   Workaround (if available)   Commercials may cut a show off a few seconds early, or another commercial may start before the previous commercial ends.  Additionally, a few seconds may be cut off from the beginning or end of a show.  This issue should be fixed in a coming release.  In the meantime, if you notice this issue happening repeatedly, please enable debug logging on your device using the steps listed under How can I report a Known Issue?\u00a0below.     Report This Issue      Google Nest Hub         Issue Description   Workaround (if available)   When giving a command to the Google Nest Hub to watch a certain channel on Sling, Google Assistant will state \"Sorry, something went wrong. When you're ready, give it another try.\"  This issue should be fixed in a coming release.  In the meantime, un-link and re-link your Sling account to the Google Nest Hub device. If this doesn't resolve the issue, try restarting your Google Nest Hub.     Report This Issue         Account and Website Issues\u00a0  Click an issue below to see more     Account Login Page      Issue Description   Workaround (if available)   Customers may experience an issue when logging in to their account on the web where after selecting Sign In,\u00a0they will be looped back to the sign-in screen and asked for their email and password again.\u00a0  This issue should be fixed in a coming release.  Instead of sling.com/signin, please visit sling.com/account\u00a0or watch.sling.com\u00a0to sign in.  Otherwise, you may need to enter your login credentials multiple times before you'll be logged in to your account.      Report This Issue      AirTV Coupons      Issue Description   Workaround (if available)   Coupons for $25 of Sling credit that came with AirTV products not\u00a0ordered through sling.com\u00a0show an expiration date of 12/31/2019. Sling will continue to honor these coupons.  To redeem, visit sling.com/airtvpromo\u00a0and follow the instructions on your screen.     Report This Issue         Resolved Issues  Click an issue below to see more.     Small screen on Roku Express+      Issue Description   Workaround (if available)       Users are reporting seeing the guide and programming on Roku Express+ devices condensed in to one corner of the screen.       This issue should be resolved in a coming release.  In the meantime, please use an HDMI cable (if available) in place of RCA cables (red, yellow, white).         Additional Questions     How can I report a Known Issue?      To report a known issue happening in your Sling TV app, you can select Report This Issue\u00a0beneath each issue to let us know. Additionally, with the app open, please visit Settings,\u00a0then Support,\u00a0and select the option to Enable Debug Logging to send a report to us.     Important Note:\u00a0If you're experiencing an issue listed here and would like to contact us, please note that agents may not have specific troubleshooting available, but will be able to log any additional details of the issue.      How long do Known Issues take to fix?      The length of time to resolve a Known Issue can vary depending on the severity of the issue, the number of people impacted, and what steps will be needed to provide a fix. As such, we don't provide estimates for timelines in resolving Known Issues, as we cannot guarantee a fix will be deployed on a given date. In some cases, we may need more information to determine the root cause of an issue.\u00a0      How will I know when Known Issues are fixed?      When a fix has been deployed, a Known Issue will move from the App and Device Issues\u00a0or Account and Website Issues\u00a0to the Resolved Issues\u00a0section of this page. Resolved issues will remain visible for 30 days after their resolution. If you can confirm the Known Issue you've experienced has been fixed and you had previously enabled\u00a0debug logging on your device, please disable\u00a0it at that time.      Are all Known Issues published?      Not all Known Issues are published, as they are resolved quickly, don't affect you at all, or there may not be a workaround available yet.\u00a0      ","description":"<div id=\"pkb-accordion\"><div><p><br></p><p>Find known issues being investigated by our team here. Resolved issues will remain visible for 30 days after their resolution. For example, if you are currently streaming ESPN on Sling TV through your Roku Device while your roommate is streaming HGTV on the XBOX One through their Sling TV account you may notice a slight lag in streaming. The reason being, more bandwidth is being used to provide both of you with video content.</p><p><br></p><p>Try testing your internet speed <a href=\"http://www.speedtest.net/\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" target=\"_blank\">here</a>. Check for <strong>download speed,\u00a0</strong>or how fast you can pull in data with your connection.   6-402 errors can appear for a number of reasons, but are most often received when you're trying to view content that has been blacked out, is expired, or is no longer available.     Choose an option that best fits what you're watching to troubleshoot or let us know about the issue:      I'm getting this error watching on a smartphone or tablet      If you're seeing error 6-402 while viewing on an Android phone or tablet, iPhone, iPad, or iPod, first make sure that location services\u00a0are enabled:    Enable location services on iPhone, iPad, or iPod Enable location services on Android phone or tablet   From the device home screen, tap Settings\u00a0  Select Privacy > Location Services > Sling TV  Ensure that While Using the App\u00a0has a check mark next to it    From the device home screen, tap the Settings\u00a0icon  Select Location > Google Location Reporting > Location Reporting  Toggle the switch to ON      If you still receive this error after enabling location services, your program may be blacked out specifically on mobile devices such as smartphones or tablets. Try viewing on your TV, or with your Google Chrome browser on PC or MAC by visiting watch.sling.com.\u00a0      I'm getting this error watching sports      If you're receiving a blackout message when trying to view an NFL, NBA, NHL, or MLB game, double-check to make sure you game isn't on another channel. Sometimes games are blacked out on a local channel or regional sports network, but not the national broadcast. Be sure to check all available channels for your game.   To enjoy the benefits of the live TV you love right at your fingertips, you don't need much!\u00a0     Check out how to get started below:      Before you start      Before you sign up for Sling TV, The quality and strength of streaming video is directly impacted by Internet speeds. When streaming content over the Internet, your connection speed is constantly changing based on the number of connected devices, as well as how fast you can receive data from your Internet Service Provider (ISP).  Visit speedtest.net from a computer connected to your home network to check your download speed, or how fast you can pull in data with your internet connection.     Check our list below to see what we recommend for a constant speed based on how you'd like to watch:   Constant speed of 3.0 Megabits per second or more - Streaming video content on portable devices such as, tablets and phones.\u00a0  Constant speed of 5.0 Megabits per second or more - Single stream of video content on a TV, PC, or Mac.\u00a0  Constant speed of 25 Megabits per second or more - Recommended for households who maintain Internet use on multiple devices.    Where can I watch Sling TV?  With Sling TV you can enjoy watching your subscription where you would like! Enjoy your favorite channels on your big screen at home, or take Sling TV with you. Simply sign in and stream on the go!    To subscribe and watch Sling TV, you must be in one of the 50 United States or Puerto Rico.   Can I use Sling TV if I live in an apartment complex, high-rise building or condominium?  You bet! Sling TV is perfect for individuals who live in an apartment. Sling TV works anywhere with a high-speed internet connection, including apartment complexes, high-rise buildings, condominiums, or homes. That\u2019s what makes Sling TV so great.   We work hard for fair deals that keep your channel costs as low as possible. Sling does not own the networks provided on our service \u2013 we have to pay programmers for the right to offer their channels to our customers. Unfortunately, programming prices have risen, and they continue to climb with no end in sight, despite our focus on negotiating fair deals. Sling is absorbing some of the cost, instead of passing everything on to you.     While there are other options out there, Sling TV remains the best value for live sports and news, and Sling is the only service that gives cord cutters the ability to customize their TV experience at an unbeatable value.     For additional answers, choose an option below:      How do I know if my price is changing?      We\u2019re communicating with all customers via email beginning December 23rd, 2019.      How much is my price changing?      For Sling base services, you will see the following changes:   Sling Orange\u00a0is now $30/month  Sling Blue\u00a0is now $30/month  Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0is now $45/month   The 4 Extras Deal\u00a0is now $12/month for Sling Orange, Sling Blue and Sling Orange + Sling Blue subscribers.     Sports Extras\u00a0is now $15/month for Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0subscribers. Sports Extra remains $10 per month as an add-on to either Sling Orange or Sling Blue.     The Total TV Deal\u00a0is now $25/month for Sling Orange + Sling Blue\u00a0subscribers. Total TV Deal remains $20 per month as an add-on to either Sling Orange or Sling Blue.     Any other extras you subscribe to, including Cloud DVR Plus, will remain unaffected.      When will my price change?      New Sling subscribers will see the updated price beginning December 23, 2019.     Existing subscribers will see the price change on their next bill after January 22, 2020.     Important Note:\u00a0If making changes to your subscription prior to January 22, 2020, you will be billed for the new prices listed above.     For subscribers with an account currently on pause, new pricing will take affect once the account is un-paused.     If you need to confirm your billing date, log in to your account at sling.com/account and check your auto-renew date, or get more information by selecting View Billing Details.      Am I getting more channels?      Since we launched in 2015, we have not raised the price of Sling Blue, although we have added 17 channels, the most recent being with the introduction of FOX News, MSNBC and HLN to the Sling Blue base service.\u00a0     We\u2019ve also added four networks to Sling Orange since the last price increase, in June 2018, and have grown one of the largest on-demand libraries with more than 126,000 titles across all Sling services, up from 12,000 titles at the end of 2015.\u00a0  Some of the latest features we\u2019ve launched include Cloud DVR Free, which includes 10 hours of Cloud DVR, plus the ability to record all Disney and ESPN channels, full player controls (like fast-forward and pause) across all recordable channels, a new ribbons to help with content discovery, like Trending Live and Recommended for You, as well as improved search and a binge-watching feature.     We continue to revamp the experiences across our platforms, including a refreshed UI on Apple TV and Roku devices, new guide on Roku devices, new search and micro guide on LG, Samsung and Xbox One devices, and \u2018launch into live\u2019 and \u2018browse while watching\u2019 features on Apple TV.     In the last half of 2019, Sling launched on Safari desktop, Android Chrome mobile, Facebook Portal and Google Nest Hub / Nest Hub Max \u2013 giving customers access to their favorite content on over 20 platforms.      Will this keep happening?      While we do everything in our power to fight for customers and keep prices low, we can\u2019t say if your price will change in the future. Programming prices continue to rise we no end in sight, but we work hard to negotiate fair deals that keep your prices as low as possible. Note:\u00a0Some games may be blacked out due to local blackout rules, or because Sling TV doesn't have the rights to broadcast a game. Impacted subscribers will not be able to watch the game unless it is also on a local broadcast network, available either through your Sling TV subscription, or with an over-the-air antenna. For more information on blackouts, please click here.     If you receive a blackout message on a Regional Sports Network you receive through Sling TV and believe this may be in error, or if that channel is missing from your guide, click here\u00a0for steps to troubleshoot the issue.     MLB Network Blackouts:\u00a0Select games will be blacked out in the markets of teams playing. In some cases, an alternate game will be shown on the MLB Network alternate channel, available in your guide. The alternate game will only\u00a0be available in those markets where the game is blacked out on the primary MLB Network channel. NBA LEAGUE PASS and NBA TEAM PASS      With NBA LEAGUE PASS and NBA TEAM PASS, you can watch the out-of-market regular season NBA matchups you've been missing. Lifelong San Antonio fan living in Brooklyn? Or maybe you're a fanatic that wants to see the biggest and best matchups every night. NBA LEAGUE PASS and NBA TEAM PASS let you follow your favorite teams, players, and matchups if you're in one city, and they're in another!\u00a0     Add NBA LEAGUE PASS or NBA TEAM PASS easily by logging in to your account at sling.com\u00a0and selecting Change Subscription.\u00a0Under Standalone Subscriptions,\u00a0select Show More.\u00a0Here, you can select NBA LEAGUE PASS to view all out-of-market games, or choose your team with NBA TEAM PASS.\u00a0        For more information on NBA LEAGUE PASS and NBA TEAM PASS, see below:    Frequently Asked Questions Can I watch my local team with NBA League Pass or NBA Team Pass? No, you'll only be able to watch out-of-market games with NBA League Pass or NBA Team Pass. For example, if you're in Memphis and want to watch the Grizzlies, their games would be blacked out for you on NBA League Pass or NBA Team Pass.What if the team I want to watch is visiting my city? If you're a die-hard Golden State fan and they're visiting your area in Washington, DC, you'd need to view the game on a regional sports network, local or national channel (if available).How am I billed for NBA League Pass or NBA Team Pass? You'll be billed $28.99 per month for the full NBA League Pass experience and $17.99 per form for NBA Team Pass, if you only want to follow a specific team. NBA League Pass and/or NBA Team Pass will automatically renew at the then-current rate unless you log in to your account online to cancel.   Important Note:\u00a0If you have NBA League Pass or NBA Team Pass as part of a prepaid plan, you will not be able to remove it until the end of the prepaid period How can I add NBA League Pass or NBA Team Pass to my subscription? It's easy! Click here\u00a0to log in to your Sling account and make changes any time you'd like.  Need additional help? Start here.How many streams can I watch NBA League Pass or NBA Team Pass on? Watch NBA League Pass and/or NBA Team Pass on up to three devices at the same time!Can I DVR games on NBA League Pass and NBA Team Pass? Absolutely! Record games like you would any other Sling programming.Will NBA League Pass and/or NBA Team Pass cancel automatically at the end of the season? No. Once the NBA regular season comes to an end, you'll need to log in to your account and remove NBA League Pass or NBA Team Pass from your subscription. Several channels across both our Sling Orange and Sling Blue base services and add-ons will show college football games this season. Check out the chart below to see what base service and/or add-on you'll need to watch college football:     Select a channel to learn more about what programming will be shown, and how to get that channel. Hit the button below to check out what games are on:     Game Finder     Schedules may not be available until closer to the beginning of the season on 8/24      What devices can I watch college football on?      College football games on Sling can be viewed on all compatible devices, including your TV, laptop, smartphone, or tablet.\u00a0     Hit the button below to view all the devices that support Sling:     Supported Devices     Ready to watch right now? Visit watch.sling.com\u00a0and start watching right from your Google Chrome browsers on PC or MAC!      Will college football games be blacked out?      Note:\u00a0Some games may be blacked out due to local blackout rules, or because Sling TV doesn't have the rights to broadcast that game. Impacted subscribers will not be able to watch the game unless it is also on a local broadcast network, available either through your Sling TV subscription, or with an over-the-air antenna.     If you receive an on-screen blackout message when trying to watch a game on ESPN, you can watch your game on ESPN3, which is included with your Sling Orange subscription. Click here for details on how to find your game on ESPN3.
